After arriving at the hotel lobby, Comrade Zhang Wei from the concierge was very enthusiastic , took me to the back kitchen of the restaurant to wrap the gift box with a disposable plastic film, but the bundling technology was not very good, and we did it for a long time. 2. The parent-child room is relatively spacious. Unfortunately, there are no facilities for children such as tents in the picture. A small bed is added next to the big bed, with a pink keiti cat blanket on it and a bear on it. My daughter likes it immediately on;

name:Dâ€uâ€oâ€yâ€a
info:Superior Twin Room
info:Stayed in January 2022
info:Business travelers
info:5 Reviews
rating:3.7
posted:Posted January 6, 2022
msg:The service staff are very good, the front desk is very enthusiastic, and the ground and stairs are cleaned by hand.
The room also has warm letters and fruit. Really attentive.

The hotel is very big
1. by car
Parking must be parked in the adjacent three-dimensional parking garage. From the parking garage to the lobby, it takes three to five minutes for the long legs and five to eight minutes for the short legs.
2. Room
First, the floors of the rooms are above the 30th floor, so you can see very far. However, if you take the elevator and go to the 30th floor before transferring, there will be a lot of time in the elevator, going up and down, not five to ten Can't do it in minutes.
In addition, it is another journey from the elevator to the front desk, and it is like walking in a maze, and you will play in circles if you are not careful.
The second is that the glass of the room is single-layered, and the floor is high, so it is ventilated! Room air conditioning can not stop. Another disadvantage of single-layer glass is that the sound is transparent. In the middle of the night, and the bang bang bang at the entrance works hard, and finally there is no sound, okay, it starts to rain, and the night rain will accompany you to sleep all night.
It can be said that it was a sleepless night, and I was very alert to the sound. It is estimated that I have been half asleep and half awake all night.
3. A lot of food around, good location
4. There is an Oshima Japanese restaurant on the second floor of the hotel, which is not bad.
